#name "MichaelWF"

struct Node { data_t val; bool marked; Node * next; } 
def @outflow[next](Node * node, data_t key) { node -> val < key } 



@graph { 
    #name "CMD(entry->val = key)"
    @node[a9 : Node*] {
        @pre-unreachable;
        @pre-emptyInflow;
        @field marked : bool = b2 / b2;
        @field val : data_t = d5 / d4;
        @field next : Node* = a12 / a12;
    }
    @constraint a12 == nullptr;
    @constraint a12 != a9;
    @constraint d4 != MIN;
    @constraint d4 != MAX;
    @constraint d4 <= MAX;
    @constraint d4 < MAX;
    @constraint d4 >= MIN;
    @constraint d4 > MIN;
    @constraint a9 != nullptr;
    @constraint d5 <= MAX;
    @constraint d5 >= MIN;
    @constraint MIN < d4;
    @constraint d4 < MAX;
    @constraint a12 == nullptr;
    @constraint a12 != a9;
    @constraint a9 != nullptr;
}
